 Responding to the discussion on the Bill, Human Resource Development Minister Kapil Sibal said that this is a historic bill which takes special care of the interests of all parties, including the creators, writers
 is vidheyak ke madhyam se rachanakaaron or saahityakaaron ko unki kriti kaa vanijyik upyog kiye jane par aaajeevan ralyati mil sakegi kyonki kai kalakaaron or rachanakaaron ko vriddhavastha main dhan kii samasya kaa saamana karnaa padaa he

 sabhi pakshon ke adhikaron kaa spasht ullekh kiya gaya he or unke sangrakshan kii bhi vyavastha kii gai he

 He said that even if folk music is used commercially, that artist will get its royalty
 isse pehle bhaajapa netaa sushamaa swaraj ne vidheyak kaa swaagat karte hue kaha ki bahut jaddojahad ke baad hi sahi lekin sarkaar ne kam se kam vidheyak ko maujuuda swaroop main sweekaar kiya he, jo kaabile tarif he

 isse pehle bhaajapa netaa sushamaa swaraj ne vidheyak kaa swaagat karte hue kaha ki bahut jaddojahad ke baad hi sahi lekin sarkaar ne kam se kam vidheyak ko maujuuda swaroop main sweekaar kiya he, jo kaabile tarif he
 He said that the standing committee of Parliament studying this bill has also worked hard to give it the current draft, which deserves congratulations
 sushamaa ne desh main geetkaar, gayak, sangeetkaar or anya kalakaaron ko unke hisse kaa laabh nahin milane se unki durdasha bayaan karte hue saath ke dashak main mashhoor gayika raheen mubarak begum kaa zikr kiya
 He told that Kuldeep Singh, who has composed a popular song like 'so Shakti Hamare Dena Daata Daan, Mana Ka Faith Weak Ho Ho Na', lives in a hut in Andheri, Mumbai, about which lyricist and Rajya Sabha member Javed Akhtar informed him
 
 bhaajapa netaa ne kuldeep singh kaa ek patr dikhaate hue kaha ki baad main unhone ek chitthee likhakar apni sthiti bataai
 During this time, lyricist Javed Akhtar was seated in the audience gallery, which has been voicing the rights of copyright to artists from time to time
 sushamaa ne kaha, ‘‘aaj sarkaar cheti he or apni jimmedaari nibhaa rahi he
 Today, the opposition also requests the entire House along with the government to pass this bill
 ’’ netaa pratipaksh ne film nirmaataaon dwaara is vidheyak par virodh kii ashankaon ke sandarbh main kaha ki 1998 main soochna or prasaaran mantri rahete unhone hi film ko udyog kaa darja diya tha
 Sushma said, "I also have a good relationship with the filmmakers
 tab main film nirmaataaon ke saath khadi thi lekin aaj un kalakaaron ke saath khadaa hone kii jarurat he jinke saath anyaay ho rahaa he
 "he said that the producers should take advantage of the artist's composition and the lyrics that are written and composed, they don't get anything, that is not right
" congress ke shashi tharur ne kaha ki rachanaatmakataa ko mapa nahin ja saktaa
 It takes 50 hours of process and hard work to write a five minute song
 tharur ne kaha ki ham is vidheyak kaa samarthan karte hue pandit sivakumar sharma, ustad amjad ali khan, e aar rahamaan or javed akhtar jaise kalakaaron ke saath ekajutata dikhaa rahe hai
 Tharoor expressed happiness over the opposition's solidarity with the bill
 jadyu netaa sharad yadav ne vidheyak kaa samarthan karte hue kaha ki sangeetkaaron, kalakaaron, rachanakaaron aadi ko is vidheyak ke jariye copirite ke daayre main laane kaa prayaas kiya gaya he jo pehle isse alag rakhe gayi the
 Yadav, while turning to Minister Sibal, also said, "I do not agree with any of your work, but i agree with this bill
" ’’ unhone yah bhi kaha ki kalakaaron ko sangrakshan to mil rahaa he lekin yah vidheyak yahi nahin ruk janaa chahie or jo lok kalakaar chhot rahe hai unka bhi dhyaan rakhaa janaa chahie
 sp's Shailendra Kumar said that this bill should have come much earlier, which has taken special care of the interests of the writers, lyricists, creators of India
 unhone kaha kuch nirmaataa iskaa virodh kar rahe hai, unhen aisa nahin karnaa chahie kyonki agar rachanaakaar yaa geetkaar nahin hoga tab filmein kaise banengi
 The comments makapa ke anup kumaar saaha ne vidheyak kaa samarthan karte hue kaha ki kai rachanaakaar or kalakaar vriddhavastha main muflisi main apana jivan vyateet karte hai, aise logon ko aaajeevan pension diya janaa chahie
 The bjd's Tathagata Satpathy called the bill unilateral, saying that it did not take care of the investors of the film and the art promoters and did not specify the stake of all parties
 charchaa main basapa ke daara singh chouhan, annadramuk ke es semalai, bipief ke es ke basumatiyaari or dramuk ke ke selvan ne bhi hissaa liya
 He said that the standing committee of Parliament studying this bill has also worked hard to give it the current draft, which deserves congratulations

 The bjd's Tathagata Satpathy called the bill unilateral, saying that it did not take care of the investors of the film and the art promoters and did not specify the stake of all parties
 charchaa main basapa ke daara singh chouhan, annadramuk ke es semalai, bipief ke es ke basumatiyaari or dramuk ke ke selvan ne bhi hissaa liya
 Sushma referred to Mubarak Begum, a famous singer in the sixties, describing her plight as songwriters, singers, musicians and other artists in the country were not benefited from her share
 unhone bataaya ki ‘itani shakti hamen dena daata, man kaa vishwaas kamjor ho naa’ jaise lokapriy geet ko sangitabaddh karne vaale kuldeep singh mumbai ke andheri main ek jhonpadi main rahete hai, jinke bare main geetkaar or rajyasabha sadsy javed akhtar ne unhen jaankaree di thi
 The BJP leader showed a letter to Kuldeep Singh saying that he later wrote a letter and stated his position
 is dauraan darshak ddeergha main geetkaar javed akhtar baithe the jo samay samay par kalakaaron ko copirite kaa adhikaar milane kii aawaaj uthaate rahe hai
 Sushma said, "today the government is alert and is carrying out its responsibility
 aaj vipaksh bhi sarkaar ke saath puure sadan se is vidheyak ko paarit karne kaa anurodh karata he
 The Leader of Opposition said in the context of fears of opposition by the filmmakers on the Bill that in 1998 he was the Minister of Information and Broadcasting and gave the film industry status
 sushamaa ne kaha, ‘‘meraa film nirmaataaon ke saath bhi madhur rishta he
 Then i stood with the filmmakers but today there is a need to stand with the actors who are being treated unfairly
 ’’ unhone kaha ki kalakaar kii rachana kaa phayda nirmaataa uthaayen or jo bol likhe, dhun banaaye use kuch nahin mili, yah thik nahin he
 Shashi Tharoor of Congress said that creativity cannot be measured
 paanch minute kaa geet likhane main 50 ghante kii prakriya or mehnat lagati he
 Tharoor said that we are showing solidarity with artists like Pandit Shivkumar Sharma, Ustad Amjad Ali Khan, AR Rahman and Javed Akhtar supporting this bill
 tharur ne vipaksh dwaara vidheyak par ekajutata pradarshit karne par khushi vyakt kii
 Supporting the bill, JDU leader Sharad Yadav said that efforts have been made to bring musicians, artists, creators etc
 under the purview of copyright through this bill which was previously kept separate from it
 yadav ne mantri sibbal kii ore mukhaatib hote hue yah bhi kaha, ‘‘aapke kisi kaam se meri sahmati nahin rahati lekin is vidheyak se main sahamat hum
 He also said that while the artists are getting patronage, this bill should not be stopped and the folk artists who are missing should also be taken care of
 sapa ke shailendra kumaar ne kaha ki yah vidheyak kaaphi pehle aana chahie tha jisamen hindustan ke sahityakaron, geetkaaron, rachanakaaron ke hiton kaa khaas khyaal rakhaa gaya he
 He said that some producers are opposing it, they should not do it because if there is no creator or lyricist then how will films be made
 tippaniyan Anup Kumar Saha of the CPI-M supported the bill, saying that many creators and artists spend their lives in Muflissi in old age, such people should be given lifetime pension
 bijd ke tathagat satpathi ne vidheyak ko ekapaksheeya qaraar dete hue kaha ki isamen filmon ke niveshkon or kala ko protsaahit karne waalon kaa khyaal nahin kiya gaya he or sabhi pakshon kii hissedari spasht nahin kii gai he

 The terrorist organization jaish-e-mohammed, which carried out the Pulwama terror attack, is being tightened
 france sarkaar ne apane desh main maujuud jaish-e-mohammad kii sampattiyon ko fries karegi
 The statement issued by the government said that terrorist Masood Azhar's organization will freeze the French assets of Jaish
 isse france ne saaf kar diya he ki wo apane desh main jaish ko pai pai ke liye mohataaj kar degaa
 a day earlier, China's veto saved Masood from being a global terrorist, but at the same time the countries had made clear that there are other ways against Masood
 France has always been and always will be by India’s side in the fight against terrorism
 France has decided to sanction Masood Azhar at the national level by freezing his assets in application of the Monetary and Financial Code

 '' We all have many precious things in the homes that thieves can steal

 In such a situation, it is very important to know how to protect your houses from thieves
 isliye redit
 Some thieves on com shared their experiences and gave people tips on keeping their homes safe
 mirar
 According to a report by com, thieves say that people fail to keep their homes safe and hence thieves find it easy to steal
 redit par gharon ko bachaae rakhane ke bare main puche gaye sawaal par kai choron ne caments kiye hai or apane suzav die hai
 The suggestions given by the thieves are as follows: 1
 aaj ke vakt main LED lits kaaphi sasti aati hai
 "if you are going out somewhere for a few days, then you can install smart lighting system in your homes
 isse aap ghar ke alag alag hisson main samay samay par lits jal jaaengi
 (eg in the kitchen at dinner, in the bedroom at bedtime, etc
)
 2
 "don't keep out your valuables that no one can easily see without entering your house
" agar aap koi nayaa tivi yaa computer kharidte hai to uske box ko dustbin ke paas na rakhen balki use puri tarah se tod den''

 4
 aap chahen to apane chote keemtee saamaan ko ek aisi jagah rakh sakate hai, jahaan chor dekhne kii bhi na soche
 For example a Fire Extinguisher 5

 6
 ghar kii khidakiyon ko yaad se band karen
 It happens many times that people leave the windows of their houses in a hurry and due to this thieves easily enter
 7
 Do not talk too much to any salesman about yourself or your home
 8
 You can also lay a trap to protect your valuables from thieves

 9

 iske baad america raashtrapati donald trump ne iskaa swaagat karte hue arabon dollar kii chini vastuon par tarriff badhaane ke nirnay ko 15 din ke liye taal diya
 Prior to this, both countries agreed to hold talks on trade war
 is khabar ke aane ke baad guuruuvaar ko subah asian share bazaar chadh gaye
 The increase in trade war between these two major economies of the world was making it difficult for the stock markets and the entire economy
 china ne kii pahalanyus agency royatres ke mutabik buudhvaar ko china ne 16 tarah ke america utpaadon par pehali baar tex par raahat diya tha
 These include some anti-cancer drugs, lubricants, animal-fish feed, etc
 ise china dwaara uthaaya gaya ek bada kadam or sakaaratmak sanket mana ja rahaa he

 i think this is a big and positive step

 'significantly, the US has decided to increase the tariff on Chinese goods from 25 to 30 percent

 strawberry fresh kriim mask-is mask ko banane se pehle sabase pehle aapako chahie strawberry puri
 In this puree, mix one teaspoon of honey with fresh cream (dry skin) and curd (oily skin)
 ab is mask ko 10 minute ke liye chehre par laga chhod den
 After this, wash the face with lukewarm water and clean it
 yah chehre se munhaason ko dur kar skin par chamak or nikhaar laata he

 Now leave this puree on your face for 15 minutes

 strawberry or chocolate mask-strawberry ko masalkar uskaa paste taiyaar kar len

 Amidst the lawyers' refusal to contest the case of gang-rape and murder of a 23-year-old para-medical student in the capital Delhi, two women judges have given suggestions for effective speedy trial of the case
 ucchtam nyaayalay kii nyaayadhish nyaayamurti gyaan sudhaa mishra ne suzav diya he ki alag-alag staron par bayaan darj karne se bachane or sunwaayee kii puri prakriya ko kam karne ke liye sakshya kanoon main sanshodhan kiya ja saktaa he
 Former Delhi High Court judge Usha Mehra said that the judge of the lower court should ensure the service of lawyers to the accused as soon as the trial starts
 nyaayamurti mishra ne kaha, meraa maananaa he ki mahilaon ke khilaaf aise jaghanya aparaadh ke maamalon ko aropiyon or peedit ke bayanon ke aadhaar par chalaaya janaa chahie, kyonki aisi prakruti ke maamle antat: police dwaara ekatrit sabooton par nirbhar hote hai
 He said, the police should record the statement of the accused and the aggrieved party before a judicial officer
 abhiyojan or bachaav paksh ke bayaan vibhinn staron par darj kyon kiye jane chahie? hamen bhartiya sakshya kanoon main parivartan karnaa chahie
 Judge Mishra said, if the statements of the accused and the victim are recorded before a judicial officer, then what is the need for a lawyer to file it in court for the second time, as has been done till now
 nyaayamurti mishra ne kaha, adaalaton ke liye keval jo cheez bachegi, vah jirah or bahes hogi or twarit adaalaton main sunwaayee aise hi tej ho sakegi
 The second time the statement is recorded in the court there is a possibility of fraud, witnesses are retracted and in many cases the main witness is killed
 samuhik balaatkaar maamle kii jaanch ke liye gathit ek-sadasyeey jaanch ayog kii pramukh nyaayamurti mehara ne haalanki pehle bhi kaha he ki kai maamalon main vakil aropiyon kaa mukadmaa ladane se inkaar kar dete hai or unhen aropiyon kaa mukadmaa ladane ke liye baadhya nahin kiya ja saktaa
 The judge of the lower court, however, has the right to provide a legal aid or appoint a jurist to defend the accused
 nyaayamurti mehara ne kaha, yadi vakil aropiyon kaa mukadmaa nahin ladane kaa faisla karte hai, to ham unhen iske liye baadhya nahin kar sakate
 He said, this is the time when the Sessions Judge hearing the case appoints the amicus curiae for the accused or ask the Delhi State Law Services Authority (DLSA) to provide legal assistance to the accused
 tippaniyan Expressing grief over the death of the Delhi gang rape victim, President of Delhi Bar Council RS Goswami said that although the council cannot make any rules by asking the lawyers not to fight the case of the accused in this case, they can ask them to be accused in such heinous cases
 May request not to appear on behalf of saket adaalat ke baar association ke upaadhyaksh arun rathi ne kaha, saket baar association 23-varshiya chaatra ke saath samuhik balaatkaar maamle main aropiyon kaa mukadmaa nahin ladane ke apane sankalp par kaayam he
 The gang rape case comes under the jurisdiction of Saket court

" unhone kaha, police ko aropiyon or peedit paksh kaa bayaan ek nyaayik adhikari ke samaksh darj karnaa chahie

 Justice Mishra said, the only thing left for the courts would be arguments and arguments and hearings in the fast courts would be speeded up like this
 duusari baar bayaan ke adaalat main darj hone se chal-kapat hone kii sambhaavna hoti he, gavaah mukar jate hai or kai maamalon main to mukhya gavaah kii hatya ho jaati he

 desh kii tex nitike liye saal 2017 kaaphi ahm rahaa
 This year not only the new tax policy Goods and Service Tax (GST) was implemented, but also many changes were made
 modi sarkaar ne jiesti ke tahat aam aadmi ko raahat dene ke liye kai utpaadon kaa rate ghataya
 The task of claiming refund has also been made easier for traders
 naye saal mengsti aam admike saath hi desh kii arthvyavastha ko raahat dene kaa kaam karegi
 Next year, where the GST Council is expected to bring petrol and diesel under the ambit of GST
 vahiin, arthvyavastha ke naye saal main jiesti ke said effect se ubharne kii ummid bhi jataai ja rahi he
 Know ahead what gifts GST can bring to you in the new year
 sasta hoga petrol-dijalanaye saal main jiestiam admiko saste petrol or dijal kaa tohfa de sakati he
 On Thursday, Bihar Finance Minister Sushil Modi also indicated this
 is saal petrol-dijal ko jiesti ke tahat laane ke liye oil ministar dharmendra pradhan or maharashtra ke mukhyamantri devendra fadanvis ne aawaaj uthaai thi
 These leaders said that GST is the only way to check the rising prices of petrol and diesel
 susheel modi kaa kahana he ki agle saal bijli bhi jiesti ke daayre main aa sakati he
 All states agree, just wait for the right time, in October, Maharashtra Finance Minister Sudhir Mungtivar said that all states have allowed petrol-diesel to be brought under the purview of GST
 unke mutabik ab in utpaadon ko iske tahat laane ke liye hamen sahi vakt kaa intjaar karnaa hoga
 It was hoped that a decision could be taken in the 23rd meeting of the GST Council, but this did not happen
 45 rupee prati litre ho jayega petroub ummid jataai ja rahi he kinaye saal main jiesti parishadpetrol or dijal ko jiesti main shaamil kar hi legi
 If this happens, you will get one liter of petrol for around Rs 45
 dijal kii keemat bhi iske aasapaas rahane kii sambhaavna he
 In fact, under the GST, the impact of continuously rising crude oil prices will be reduced
 sasta hoga ghar khareednaavitt mantri arun jetali kah chuke hai ki real estate ko jiesti ke daayre main laayaa ja saktaa he
 Sushil Modi has also reiterated this
 jetali ke mutabik isse na sirf aam aadmi ko sasta ghar kharidne main madad milegi, balki yah kar chori par bhi lagaam kasne main madadgaar sabit hoga
 Tax evasion will be curbed, according to the maximum tax evasion in the real estate sector
 agar ise jiesti ke daayre main laa diya jaataa he, to kar chori par kaaphi had tak lagaam kasi ja sakati he
 On this also, the decision was being expected to be taken in the 23rd meeting of the GST Council, but this did not happen
 iske baad naye saal main real estate ko jiesti ke tahat laana tay he
 Tax slabs will be reduced in the coming new year, under GST, the tax slab will be reduced to just two
 vitt mantri arun jetali kah chuke hai ki jiesti parishad kii agali baithak main maujuuda 5 tex slab ko 2 main hi simit kiya ja saktaa he
